<a id="175" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="180" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="187" href="univalent-foundations.html" class="Module">univalent-foundations</a> <a id="209" class="Keyword">public</a>

## Groups in Univalent Mathematics

We first introduce semigroups, and then groups. We do this because the
category of groups is a full subcategory of the category of semigroups.
In particular, it is a proposition for a semigroup to be a group. Therefore
this approach gives us in a straightforward way that equality of groups is
equality of semigroups. This will be useful in showing that group isomorphisms
are equivalent to identifications of groups.

<a id="6403" class="Comment">{- Next, we prove the that the laws for a category hold for group homomorphisms,
   i.e., we show that composition is associative and satisfies the left and
   right unit laws. Before we show that these laws hold, we will characterize
   the identity type of the types of semigroup homomorphisms and group 
   homomorphisms. -}</a>

<a id="associative-comp-hom-Semigroup"></a><a id="6732" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#6732" class="Function">associative-comp-hom-Semigroup</a> <a id="6763" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="22843" class="Comment">--------------------------------------------------------------------------------</a>

<a id="22925" class="Comment">{- The property that a monoid is a group is just the property that the monoid
   that every element is invertible, i.e., it comes equipped with an inverse
   operation that satisfies the left and right inverse laws. -}</a>

    <a id="35923" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#35850" class="Function">is-contr-total-iso-Group</a> <a id="35948" class="Symbol">=</a>

        <a id="35980" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="35982" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="35984" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35985" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#23569" class="Function">Group</a> <a id="35991" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#35316" class="Bound">l</a><a id="35992" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35994" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35995" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="35998" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#35328" class="Bound">G</a><a id="35999" class="Symbol">))</a>
        <a id="36010" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="36012" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-pair-types.html#6804" class="Function">equiv-tot</a> <a id="36022" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#35586" class="Function">extensionality-Group&#39;</a><a id="36043" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="36053" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="36055" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#1970" class="Function">is-contr-total-path</a> <a id="36075" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#35328" class="Bound">G</a><a id="36076" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="is-category-Group"></a><a id="36079" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36079" class="Function">is-category-Group</a> <a id="36097" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36099" href="category-theory.large-categories.html#878" class="Function">is-category-Large-Precat</a> <a id="36124" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#33560" class="Function">Group-Large-Precat</a>
<a id="36143" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36079" class="Function">is-category-Group</a> <a id="36161" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36161" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="36163" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="36167" href="foundation-core.fundamental-theorem-of-identity-types.html#1888" class="Function">fundamental-theorem-id</a> <a id="36190" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36161" class="Bound">G</a>
    <a id="36196" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="36198" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#35352" class="Function">id-iso-Group</a> <a id="36211" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36161" class="Bound">G</a><a id="36212" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="36218" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="36220" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#35850" class="Function">is-contr-total-iso-Group</a> <a id="36245" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36161" class="Bound">G</a><a id="36246" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="36252" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="36254" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#35453" class="Function">iso-eq-Group</a> <a id="36267" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36161" class="Bound">G</a><a id="36268" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="eq-iso-Group"></a><a id="36271" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36271" class="Function">eq-iso-Group</a> <a id="36284" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36286" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36287" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36287" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="36289" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36291" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="36296" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36298" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36299" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36299" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="36301" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36301" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="36303" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36305" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#23569" class="Function">Group</a> <a id="36311" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36287" class="Bound">l</a><a id="36312" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36314" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36316" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#34448" class="Function">type-iso-Group</a> <a id="36331" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36299" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="36333" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36301" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="36335" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36337" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="36340" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36299" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="36342" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36301" class="Bound">H</a>
<a id="36344" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36271" class="Function">eq-iso-Group</a> <a id="36357" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36357" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="36359" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36359" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="36361" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36363" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#4173" class="Function">map-inv-is-equiv</a> <a id="36380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36381" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36079" class="Function">is-category-Group</a> <a id="36399" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36357" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="36401" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36359" class="Bound">H</a><a id="36402" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="Group-Large-Cat"></a><a id="36405" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36405" class="Function">Group-Large-Cat</a> <a id="36421" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36423" href="category-theory.large-categories.html#1110" class="Record">Large-Cat</a> <a id="36433" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="36438" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="36441" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36441" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="36444" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36444" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="36447" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36449" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36441" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="36452" href="Agda.Primitive.html#810" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="36454" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36444" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="36456" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="36458" href="category-theory.large-categories.html#1222" class="Field">precat-Large-Cat</a> <a id="36475" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36405" class="Function">Group-Large-Cat</a> <a id="36491" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36493" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#33560" class="Function">Group-Large-Precat</a>
<a id="36512" href="category-theory.large-categories.html#1262" class="Field">is-category-Large-Cat</a> <a id="36534" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36405" class="Function">Group-Large-Cat</a> <a id="36550" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36552" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36079" class="Function">is-category-Group</a>
</pre>### Examples of groups

#### The group of integers

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ℤ-Semigroup"></a><a id="36634" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36634" class="Function">ℤ-Semigroup</a> <a id="36646" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36648" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#956" class="Function">Semigroup</a> <a id="36658" href="Agda.Primitive.html#764" class="Primitive">lzero</a>
<a id="36664" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="36668" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36634" class="Function">ℤ-Semigroup</a> <a id="36680" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36682" href="elementary-number-theory.equality-integers.html#3338" class="Function">ℤ-Set</a>
<a id="36688" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="36692" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36693" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36697" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36634" class="Function">ℤ-Semigroup</a><a id="36708" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36710" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36712" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1489" class="Function">add-ℤ</a>
<a id="36718" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36723" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36727" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36634" class="Function">ℤ-Semigroup</a><a id="36738" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36740" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36742" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#5297" class="Function">associative-add-ℤ</a>

<a id="ℤ-Group"></a><a id="36761" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36761" class="Function">ℤ-Group</a> <a id="36769" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36771" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#23569" class="Function">Group</a> <a id="36777" href="Agda.Primitive.html#764" class="Primitive">lzero</a>
<a id="36783" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="36787" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36761" class="Function">ℤ-Group</a> <a id="36795" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36797" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36634" class="Function">ℤ-Semigroup</a>

<a id="36842" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="36846" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36847" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36852" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="36856" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36857" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36861" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36761" class="Function">ℤ-Group</a><a id="36868" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="36872" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36874" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1948" class="Function">left-unit-law-add-ℤ</a>
<a id="36894" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36898" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36899" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36903" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36904" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="36908" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36909" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36913" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36761" class="Function">ℤ-Group</a><a id="36920" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="36924" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36926" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#2042" class="Function">right-unit-law-add-ℤ</a>
<a id="36947" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="36951" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36952" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36956" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36957" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36961" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36761" class="Function">ℤ-Group</a><a id="36968" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="36971" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36973" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#3749" class="Function">neg-ℤ</a>
<a id="36979" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="36983" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36984" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36988" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36989" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36993" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36994" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="36998" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36761" class="Function">ℤ-Group</a><a id="37005" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="37009" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37011" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#7226" class="Function">left-inverse-law-add-ℤ</a>
<a id="37034" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37038" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37039" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37043" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37044" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37048" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37049" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37053" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#36761" class="Function">ℤ-Group</a><a id="37060" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="37064" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37066" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#7735" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-ℤ</a>

#### The group of integers modulo k

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ℤ-Mod-Semigroup"></a><a id="37140" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37140" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Semigroup</a> <a id="37156" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37158" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37159" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37159" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="37161" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37163" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1444" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="37164" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37166" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="37168" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#956" class="Function">Semigroup</a> <a id="37178" href="Agda.Primitive.html#764" class="Primitive">lzero</a>
<a id="37184" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37188" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37189" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37140" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Semigroup</a> <a id="37205" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37205" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37206" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37208" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37210" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#4485" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Set</a> <a id="37220" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37205" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="37222" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37226" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37227" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37231" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37232" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37140" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Semigroup</a> <a id="37248" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37248" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37249" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="37252" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37254" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#6417" class="Function">add-ℤ-Mod</a> <a id="37264" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37248" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="37266" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37270" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37271" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37275" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37276" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37140" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Semigroup</a> <a id="37292" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37292" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37293" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="37296" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37298" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#8313" class="Function">associative-add-ℤ-Mod</a> <a id="37320" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37292" class="Bound">k</a>

<a id="ℤ-Mod-Group"></a><a id="37323" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37323" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Group</a> <a id="37335" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37337" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37338" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37338" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="37340" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37342" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1444" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="37343" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37345" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="37347" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#23569" class="Function">Group</a> <a id="37353" href="Agda.Primitive.html#764" class="Primitive">lzero</a>
<a id="37359" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37363" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37364" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37323" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Group</a> <a id="37376" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37376" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37377" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37379" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37381" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37140" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Semigroup</a> <a id="37397" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37376" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="37399" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37403" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37404" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37408" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37409" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37414" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37323" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Group</a> <a id="37426" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37426" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37427" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="37431" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37433" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#3563" class="Function">zero-ℤ-Mod</a> <a id="37444" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37426" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="37446" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37450" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37451" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37455" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37456" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37460" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37461" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37465" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37466" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37323" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Group</a> <a id="37478" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37478" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37479" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="37484" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37486" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#8741" class="Function">left-unit-law-add-ℤ-Mod</a> <a id="37510" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37478" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="37512" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37516" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37517" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37521" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37522" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37527" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37531" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37532" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37323" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Group</a> <a id="37544" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37544" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37545" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="37550" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37552" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#8942" class="Function">right-unit-law-add-ℤ-Mod</a> <a id="37577" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37544" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="37579" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37583" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37584" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37588" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37589" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37593" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37594" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37323" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Group</a> <a id="37606" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37606" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37607" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="37611" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37613" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#7880" class="Function">neg-ℤ-Mod</a> <a id="37623" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37606" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="37625" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="37629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37630" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37634" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37635" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37639" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37640" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37644" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37645" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37323" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Group</a> <a id="37657" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37657" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37658" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="37663" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37665" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#9148" class="Function">left-inverse-law-add-ℤ-Mod</a> <a id="37692" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37657" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="37694" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37698" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37699" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37703" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37704" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37708" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37709" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="37713" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37714" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37323" class="Function">ℤ-Mod-Group</a> <a id="37726" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37726" class="Bound">k</a><a id="37727" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="37732" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37734" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic.html#9378" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-ℤ-Mod</a> <a id="37762" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#37726" class="Bound">k</a>
</pre>
#### The group of loops in a 1-type

<a id="42739" class="Comment">{- We show that group homomorphisms preserve inverses. -}</a>
